<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Lobe i18n</h1><a id="user-content-lobe-i18n" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Lobe i18n" href="#lobe-i18n"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Lobe i18n is a CLI workflow tool that uses ChatGPT for automated i18n.</p>
<p dir="auto">English ・ <a href="/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox/blob/master/packages/lobe-i18n/README.zh-CN.md">简体中文</a> ・ <a href="/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox/blob/master/packages/lobe-i18n/CHANGELOG.md">Changelog</a> · <a href="https://github.com/canisminor1990/lobe-commit/issues/new/choose">Report Bug</a> · <a href="https://github.com/canisminor1990/lobe-commit/issues/new/choose">Request Feature</a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">✨ Features</h2><a id="user-content--features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ✨ Features" href="#-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul class="contains-task-list">
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Completed task" checked=""> 🤖 Utilize ChatGPT for automated i18n translation</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Completed task" checked=""> ✂️ Support automatic splitting of large files without worrying about ChatGPT token limits.</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Completed task" checked=""> ♻️ Support incremental i18n updates, automatically extract new content based on <code>entry</code> files.</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Completed task" checked=""> 🗂️ Support single file mode <code>en_US.json</code> and folder mode <code>en_US/common.json</code> to work perfectly with <code>i18next</code>.</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Completed task" checked=""> 🌲 Support <code>flat</code> and <code>tree</code> structure for locale files.</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Completed task" checked=""> 🛠️ Support customizing OpenAI models, API proxies, temperature and topP.</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Completed task" checked=""> 📝 Support automated i18n translation of <code>Markdown</code> files.</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Completed task" checked=""> 🔍 Support linting translation files for language correctness using eld.</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📦 Installation</h2><a id="user-content--installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📦 Installation" href="#-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To install Lobe i18n, run the following command:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npm install -g @lobehub/i18n-cli"><pre>npm install -g @lobehub/i18n-cli</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-important" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-report mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 1.75C0 .784.784 0 1.75 0h12.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v9.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 13H8.06l-2.573 2.573A1.458 1.458 0 0 1 3 14.543V13H1.75A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 11.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v9.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h2a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.19l2.72-2.72a.749.749 0 0 1 .53-.22h6.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-9.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Zm7 2.25v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 9a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Important</p><p dir="auto">Please make sure you have <code>Node.js</code> version <strong>&gt;= 18</strong>.</p>
</div>

</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🤯 Usage</h2><a id="user-content--usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🤯 Usage" href="#-usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 1: Initialize Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-step-1-initialize-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 1: Initialize Configuration" href="#step-1-initialize-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To initialize the Lobe i18n configuration, run the following command:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ lobe-i18n -o # or use the full flag --option"><pre>$ lobe-i18n -o <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> or use the full flag --option</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 2: Run Translation Commands</h3><a id="user-content-step-2-run-translation-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 2: Run Translation Commands" href="#step-2-run-translation-commands"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This command will guide you through creating a configuration file step by step.</p>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, you can manually create a configuration file in one of the formats supported by <a href="https://github.com/cosmiconfig/cosmiconfig">cosmiconfig</a> (see <a href="#configuration">Configuration</a> below).</p>
<p dir="auto">Here's an example of a configuration file (<code>.i18nrc.js</code>):<br>
This example demonstrates how to generate <code>locales/zh_CN.json</code> and <code>locales/ja_JP.json</code> automatically based on <code>locales/en_US.json</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const { defineConfig } = require('@lobehub/i18n-cli');

module.exports = defineConfig({
  entry: 'locales/en_US.json',
  entryLocale: 'en_US',
  output: 'locales',
  outputLocales: ['zh_CN', 'ja_JP'],
});"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> defineConfig <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'@lobehub/i18n-cli'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-smi">module</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">exports</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">defineConfig</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">entry</span>: <span class="pl-s">'locales/en_US.json'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">entryLocale</span>: <span class="pl-s">'en_US'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">output</span>: <span class="pl-s">'locales'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">outputLocales</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'zh_CN'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'ja_JP'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-important" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-report mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 1.75C0 .784.784 0 1.75 0h12.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v9.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 13H8.06l-2.573 2.573A1.458 1.458 0 0 1 3 14.543V13H1.75A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 11.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v9.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h2a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.19l2.72-2.72a.749.749 0 0 1 .53-.22h6.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-9.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Zm7 2.25v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 9a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Important</p><p dir="auto">To use AI auto-generation, you need to fill in the <a href="https://platform.openai.com/account/api-keys" rel="nofollow">OpenAI Token</a> in the settings.</p>
</div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Translate Locale files
$ lobe-i18n # or $ lobe-i18n locale

# Translate Markdown files
$ lobe-i18n md

# Lint translation files for language correctness
$ lobe-i18n lint # or $ lobe-i18n --lint

# Run i18n translation and markdown translation simultaneously
$ lobe-i18n --with-md

# Specify the configuration file
$ lobe-i18n -c './custom-config.js' # or use the full flag --config"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Translate Locale files</span>
$ lobe-i18n <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> or $ lobe-i18n locale</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Translate Markdown files</span>
$ lobe-i18n md

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Lint translation files for language correctness</span>
$ lobe-i18n lint <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> or $ lobe-i18n --lint</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run i18n translation and markdown translation simultaneously</span>
$ lobe-i18n --with-md

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Specify the configuration file</span>
$ lobe-i18n -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>./custom-config.js<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> or use the full flag --config</span></pre></div>
<br>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuration" href="#configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can choose any configuration method in <a href="https://github.com/cosmiconfig/cosmiconfig">cosmiconfig</a> format</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>i18n</code> property in <code>package.json</code></li>
<li><code>.i18nrc</code> file in JSON or YAML format</li>
<li><code>.i18nrc.json</code>, <code>.i18nrc.yaml</code>, <code>.i18nrc.yml</code>, <code>.i18nrc.js</code>, <code>.i18nrc.cjs</code></li>
<li><code>defineConfig</code> provides a secure definition method that can be imported from <code>@lobehub/i18n-cli</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-tip" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-light-bulb mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M8 1.5c-2.363 0-4 1.69-4 3.75 0 .984.424 1.625.984 2.304l.214.253c.223.264.47.556.673.848.284.411.537.896.621 1.49a.75.75 0 0 1-1.484.211c-.04-.282-.163-.547-.37-.847a8.456 8.456 0 0 0-.542-.68c-.084-.1-.173-.205-.268-.32C3.201 7.75 2.5 6.766 2.5 5.25 2.5 2.31 4.863 0 8 0s5.5 2.31 5.5 5.25c0 1.516-.701 2.5-1.328 3.259-.095.115-.184.22-.268.319-.207.245-.383.453-.541.681-.208.3-.33.565-.37.847a.751.751 0 0 1-1.485-.212c.084-.593.337-1.078.621-1.489.203-.292.45-.584.673-.848.075-.088.147-.173.213-.253.561-.679.985-1.32.985-2.304 0-2.06-1.637-3.75-4-3.75ZM5.75 12h4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5ZM6 15.25a.75.75 0 0 1 .75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75Z"></path></svg>Tip</p>
<p dir="auto">This project provides a secure definition method <code>defineConfig</code> that can be imported from <code>@lobehub/i18n-cli</code></p>
</div>
<br>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Environment Variable</h3><a id="user-content-environment-variable" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Environment Variable" href="#environment-variable"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example 1 <code>.i18nrc.js</code></h4><a id="user-content-example-1-i18nrcjs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example 1 .i18nrc.js" href="#example-1-i18nrcjs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const { defineConfig } = require('@lobehub/i18n-cli');

module.exports = defineConfig({
  entry: 'locales/en_US.json',
  entryLocale: 'en_US',
  output: 'locales',
  outputLocales: ['zh_CN', 'ja_JP'],
});"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> defineConfig <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'@lobehub/i18n-cli'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-smi">module</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">exports</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">defineConfig</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">entry</span>: <span class="pl-s">'locales/en_US.json'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">entryLocale</span>: <span class="pl-s">'en_US'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">output</span>: <span class="pl-s">'locales'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">outputLocales</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'zh_CN'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'ja_JP'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example 2 <code>.i18nrc.json</code></h4><a id="user-content-example-2-i18nrcjson" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example 2 .i18nrc.json" href="#example-2-i18nrcjson"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

  }

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example 4 - Enable Immediate Save</h4><a id="user-content-example-4---enable-immediate-save" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example 4 - Enable Immediate Save" href="#example-4---enable-immediate-save"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const { defineConfig } = require('@lobehub/i18n-cli');

module.exports = defineConfig({
  entry: 'locales/en_US.json',
  entryLocale: 'en_US',
  output: 'locales',
  outputLocales: ['zh_CN', 'ja_JP'],
  saveImmediately: true, // Save results immediately after each chunk completes
  concurrency: 5,
  temperature: 0.3,
});"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> defineConfig <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'@lobehub/i18n-cli'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-smi">module</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">exports</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">defineConfig</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">entry</span>: <span class="pl-s">'locales/en_US.json'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">entryLocale</span>: <span class="pl-s">'en_US'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">output</span>: <span class="pl-s">'locales'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">outputLocales</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'zh_CN'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'ja_JP'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">saveImmediately</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Save results immediately after each chunk completes</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">concurrency</span>: <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">temperature</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0.3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-tip" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-light-bulb mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M8 1.5c-2.363 0-4 1.69-4 3.75 0 .984.424 1.625.984 2.304l.214.253c.223.264.47.556.673.848.284.411.537.896.621 1.49a.75.75 0 0 1-1.484.211c-.04-.282-.163-.547-.37-.847a8.456 8.456 0 0 0-.542-.68c-.084-.1-.173-.205-.268-.32C3.201 7.75 2.5 6.766 2.5 5.25 2.5 2.31 4.863 0 8 0s5.5 2.31 5.5 5.25c0 1.516-.701 2.5-1.328 3.259-.095.115-.184.22-.268.319-.207.245-.383.453-.541.681-.208.3-.33.565-.37.847a.751.751 0 0 1-1.485-.212c.084-.593.337-1.078.621-1.489.203-.292.45-.584.673-.848.075-.088.147-.173.213-.253.561-.679.985-1.32.985-2.304 0-2.06-1.637-3.75-4-3.75ZM5.75 12h4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5ZM6 15.25a.75.75 0 0 1 .75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75Z"></path></svg>Tip</p>
<p dir="auto">Enabling <code>saveImmediately</code> allows you to see translation progress in real-time and provides better fault tolerance. If the translation process is interrupted, completed chunks won't be lost.</p>
</div>
<div align="right" dir="auto">
<p dir="auto"><a href="#readme-top"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/49d3e15522e0b9750d3de243d91e5452dda84123b6003000a468c58b5bb0252e/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d4241434b5f544f5f544f502d3135313531353f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-BACK_TO_TOP-151515?style=flat-square" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">File Structure Selection</h3><a id="user-content-file-structure-selection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: File Structure Selection" href="#file-structure-selection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">There are two types of file structures supported: <code>flat</code> and <code>tree</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Flat Structure</h4><a id="user-content-flat-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Flat Structure" href="#flat-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A flat structure means that all translations for different languages are stored in a single file, as shown below:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="- locales
  - en_US.json
  - ja_JP.json
  - zh_CN.json
  - ..."><pre class="notranslate"><code>- locales
  - en_US.json
  - ja_JP.json
  - zh_CN.json
  - ...
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-tip" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-light-bulb mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M8 1.5c-2.363 0-4 1.69-4 3.75 0 .984.424 1.625.984 2.304l.214.253c.223.264.47.556.673.848.284.411.537.896.621 1.49a.75.75 0 0 1-1.484.211c-.04-.282-.163-.547-.37-.847a8.456 8.456 0 0 0-.542-.68c-.084-.1-.173-.205-.268-.32C3.201 7.75 2.5 6.766 2.5 5.25 2.5 2.31 4.863 0 8 0s5.5 2.31 5.5 5.25c0 1.516-.701 2.5-1.328 3.259-.095.115-.184.22-.268.319-.207.245-.383.453-.541.681-.208.3-.33.565-.37.847a.751.751 0 0 1-1.485-.212c.084-.593.337-1.078.621-1.489.203-.292.45-.584.673-.848.075-.088.147-.173.213-.253.561-.679.985-1.32.985-2.304 0-2.06-1.637-3.75-4-3.75ZM5.75 12h4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5ZM6 15.25a.75.75 0 0 1 .75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75Z"></path></svg>Tip</p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>flat structure</code> requires configuring the <code>entry</code> property in the configuration file to the corresponding JSON file <a href="/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox/blob/master/packages/lobe-i18n/examples/locale/flat/.i18nrc.cjs">Example</a></p>
</div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;entry&quot;: &quot;locales/en.json&quot;,
  &quot;entryLocale&quot;: &quot;en_US&quot;,
  &quot;output&quot;: &quot;locales&quot;,
  &quot;outputLocales&quot;: [&quot;zh_CN&quot;, &quot;ja_JP&quot;]
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"entry"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>locales/en.json<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"entryLocale"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>en_US<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"output"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>locales<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"outputLocales"</span>: [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>zh_CN<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ja_JP<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>]
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tree Structure</h4><a id="user-content-tree-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tree Structure" href="#tree-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A tree structure means that the translations for each language are stored in separate language folders, as shown below:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="- locales
  - en_US
    - common.json
    - header.json
    - subfolder
      - ...
  - ja_JP
    - common.json
    - header.json
    - subfolder
      - ...
  - zh_CN
    - common.json
    - header.json
    - subfolder
      - ..."><pre class="notranslate"><code>- locales
  - en_US
    - common.json
    - header.json
    - subfolder
      - ...
  - ja_JP
    - common.json
    - header.json
    - subfolder
      - ...
  - zh_CN
    - common.json
    - header.json
    - subfolder
      - ...
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-tip" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-light-bulb mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M8 1.5c-2.363 0-4 1.69-4 3.75 0 .984.424 1.625.984 2.304l.214.253c.223.264.47.556.673.848.284.411.537.896.621 1.49a.75.75 0 0 1-1.484.211c-.04-.282-.163-.547-.37-.847a8.456 8.456 0 0 0-.542-.68c-.084-.1-.173-.205-.268-.32C3.201 7.75 2.5 6.766 2.5 5.25 2.5 2.31 4.863 0 8 0s5.5 2.31 5.5 5.25c0 1.516-.701 2.5-1.328 3.259-.095.115-.184.22-.268.319-.207.245-.383.453-.541.681-.208.3-.33.565-.37.847a.751.751 0 0 1-1.485-.212c.084-.593.337-1.078.621-1.489.203-.292.45-.584.673-.848.075-.088.147-.173.213-.253.561-.679.985-1.32.985-2.304 0-2.06-1.637-3.75-4-3.75ZM5.75 12h4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5ZM6 15.25a.75.75 0 0 1 .75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75Z"></path></svg>Tip</p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>tree structure</code> requires configuring the <code>entry</code> property in the configuration file to the corresponding folder <a href="/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox/blob/master/packages/lobe-i18n/examples/locale/tree/.i18nrc.cjs">Example</a></p>
</div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;entry&quot;: &quot;locales/en_US&quot;,
  &quot;entryLocale&quot;: &quot;en_US&quot;,
  &quot;output&quot;: &quot;locales&quot;,
  &quot;outputLocales&quot;: [&quot;zh_CN&quot;, &quot;ja_JP&quot;]
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"entry"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>locales/en_US<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"entryLocale"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>en_US<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"output"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>locales<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"outputLocales"</span>: [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>zh_CN<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ja_JP<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>]
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running</h3><a id="user-content-running" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running" href="#running"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use the <code>lobe-i18n</code> command to generate i18n files automatically:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ lobe-i18n"><pre>$ lobe-i18n</pre></div>
<div align="right" dir="auto">
<p dir="auto"><a href="#readme-top"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/49d3e15522e0b9750d3de243d91e5452dda84123b6003000a468c58b5bb0252e/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d4241434b5f544f5f544f502d3135313531353f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-BACK_TO_TOP-151515?style=flat-square" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📝 Markdown Configuration</h2><a id="user-content--markdown-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📝 Markdown Configuration" href="#-markdown-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>

<tr>
<td>entry</td>

<td><code>string[]</code></td>
<td><code>[]</code></td>
<td>Entry file or folder, supports <code>glob</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>entryLocale</td>
<td></td>
<td><code>string</code></td>
<td><em>Inherit parent locale</em></td>
<td>Reference language for translation</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>entryExtension</td>
<td></td>
<td><code>string</code></td>
<td><code>.md</code></td>
<td>Entry file extension</td>
</tr>

<td>exclude</td>
<td></td>
<td><code>string[]</code></td>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>outputExtensions</code></h4><a id="user-content-outputextensions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: outputExtensions" href="#outputextensions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">By default, the translated file names are generated as <code>.{locale}.md</code>. You can customize the output file extensions with <code>outputExtensions</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p>
<p dir="auto">In the example below, the entry file extension is <code>.zh-CN.md</code>, but we want the output file extension for the <code>en-US</code> translation to be <code>.md</code>, while other languages keep the default extensions.</p>
</div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="module.exports = {
  markdown: {
    entry: ['./README.zh-CN.md', './docs/**/*.zh-CN.md'],
    entryLocale: 'zh-CN',
    entryExtension: '.zh-CN.md',
    outputLocales: ['en-US', 'ja-JP'],
    outputExtensions: (locale, { getDefaultExtension }) =&gt; {
      if (locale === 'en-US') return '.md';
      return getDefaultExtension(locale);
    },
  },
};"><pre><span class="pl-smi">module</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">exports</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">markdown</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">entry</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'./README.zh-CN.md'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'./docs/**/*.zh-CN.md'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">entryLocale</span>: <span class="pl-s">'zh-CN'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">entryExtension</span>: <span class="pl-s">'.zh-CN.md'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">outputLocales</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'en-US'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'ja-JP'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-en">outputExtensions</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">locale</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> getDefaultExtension <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">locale</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'en-US'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">'.md'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">getDefaultExtension</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">locale</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><code>outputExtensions</code> supports the following <code>props</code>:</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="interface OutputExtensionsProps {
  /**
   * @description The locale of the translated file to output
   */
  locale: string;
  config: {
    /**
     * @description The content of the translated file to input
     */
    fileContent: string;
    /**
     * @description The path of the translated file to input
     */
    filePath: string;
    /**
     * @description The default method for generating extensions
     */
    getDefaultExtension: (locale: string) =&gt; string;
  };
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">interface</span> <span class="pl-smi">OutputExtensionsProps</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c">   * <span class="pl-k">@description</span> The locale of the translated file to output</span>
<span class="pl-c">   */</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">locale</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">config</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c">     * <span class="pl-k">@description</span> The content of the translated file to input</span>
<span class="pl-c">     */</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">fileContent</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c">     * <span class="pl-k">@description</span> The path of the translated file to input</span>
<span class="pl-c">     */</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">filePath</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c">     * <span class="pl-k">@description</span> The default method for generating extensions</span>
<span class="pl-c">     */</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">getDefaultExtension</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">locale</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>mode</code></h4><a id="user-content-mode" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: mode" href="#mode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>mode</code> is used to specify the translation mode, which supports two modes and custom generation modes.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>string</code> - Translates the complete <code>markdown</code> content.</li>
<li><code>mdast</code> - Parses the text with <code>mdast</code> structure and translates the <code>text value</code> content. To translate code blocks, you need to enable <code>translateCode</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p>
<p dir="auto">In <code>mdast</code> mode, the content to be translated will be reduced to a minimum, removing most markdown syntax structures and links.
This mode can greatly reduce token consumption, but it may result in inaccurate translation results.</p>
</div>
<div align="right" dir="auto">
<p dir="auto"><a href="#readme-top"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/49d3e15522e0b9750d3de243d91e5452dda84123b6003000a468c58b5bb0252e/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d4241434b5f544f5f544f502d3135313531353f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-BACK_TO_TOP-151515?style=flat-square" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">File Structure</h3><a id="user-content-file-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: File Structure" href="#file-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The translated files will be generated in the same directory as the entry file, with the corresponding language suffix added to the extension:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="- README.md
- README.zh-CN.md
	- docs
		- usage.md
		- usage.zh-CN.md
		- subfolder
            - ..."><pre class="notranslate"><code>- README.md
- README.zh-CN.md
	- docs
		- usage.md
		- usage.zh-CN.md
		- subfolder
            - ...
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-tip" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-light-bulb mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M8 1.5c-2.363 0-4 1.69-4 3.75 0 .984.424 1.625.984 2.304l.214.253c.223.264.47.556.673.848.284.411.537.896.621 1.49a.75.75 0 0 1-1.484.211c-.04-.282-.163-.547-.37-.847a8.456 8.456 0 0 0-.542-.68c-.084-.1-.173-.205-.268-.32C3.201 7.75 2.5 6.766 2.5 5.25 2.5 2.31 4.863 0 8 0s5.5 2.31 5.5 5.25c0 1.516-.701 2.5-1.328 3.259-.095.115-.184.22-.268.319-.207.245-.383.453-.541.681-.208.3-.33.565-.37.847a.751.751 0 0 1-1.485-.212c.084-.593.337-1.078.621-1.489.203-.292.45-.584.673-.848.075-.088.147-.173.213-.253.561-.679.985-1.32.985-2.304 0-2.06-1.637-3.75-4-3.75ZM5.75 12h4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5ZM6 15.25a.75.75 0 0 1 .75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75Z"></path></svg>Tip</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox/blob/master/packages/lobe-i18n/examples/markdown/.i18nrc.cjs">Example</a></p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running</h3><a id="user-content-running-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running" href="#running-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use the <code>lobe-i18n md</code> command to automate the generation of i18n files:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ lobe-i18n md"><pre>$ lobe-i18n md</pre></div>
<div align="right" dir="auto">
<p dir="auto"><a href="#readme-top"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/49d3e15522e0b9750d3de243d91e5452dda84123b6003000a468c58b5bb0252e/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d4241434b5f544f5f544f502d3135313531353f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-BACK_TO_TOP-151515?style=flat-square" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">⌨️ Local Development</h2><a id="user-content-️-local-development" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ⌨️ Local Development" href="#️-local-development"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can use Github Codespaces for online development:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://codespaces.new/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://github.com/codespaces/badge.svg" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, you can clone the repository and run the following command for local development:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://bun.sh" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/25f28e161904a25aead369b2968902f04daebafbc1b207c6def144fb7ae4d8ae/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d737065656475702532307769746825323062756e2d626c61636b3f6c6f676f3d62756e267374796c653d666f722d7468652d6261646765" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-speedup%20with%20bun-black?logo=bun&amp;style=for-the-badge" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ git clone https://github.com/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox.git
$ cd lobe-cli-toolbox
$ bun install
$ cd packages/lobe-i18n
$ bun dev"><pre>$ git clone https://github.com/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox.git
$ <span class="pl-c1">cd</span> lobe-cli-toolbox
$ bun install
$ <span class="pl-c1">cd</span> packages/lobe-i18n
$ bun dev</pre></div>
<div align="right" dir="auto">
<p dir="auto"><a href="#readme-top"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/49d3e15522e0b9750d3de243d91e5452dda84123b6003000a468c58b5bb0252e/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d4241434b5f544f5f544f502d3135313531353f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-BACK_TO_TOP-151515?style=flat-square" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🤝 Contributing</h2><a id="user-content--contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🤝 Contributing" href="#-contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We welcome contributions in all forms. If you're interested in contributing code, you can check our GitHub <a href="https://github.com/lobehub/lobe-cli-toolbox/issues">Issues</a>, show off your skills, and demonstrate your ideas.</p>
